  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ba556227-7caa-4f06-9771-88032bae5043'

  <span id="freeText13444787537621502709" style="display:none">Graham Russell and I weren’t made for one another.<br /><br />I was driven by emotion; he was apathetic. I dreamed while he lived in nightmares. I cried when he had no tears to shed.<br /><br />Despite his frozen heart and my readiness to run, we sometimes shared seconds. Seconds when our eyes locked and we saw each other’s secrets. Seconds when his lips tasted my fears, and I breathed in his pains. Seconds when we both imagined what it would be like to love one another.<br /><br />Those seconds left us floating, but when reality knocked us sideways, gravity forced us to descend.<br /><br />Graham Russell wasn’t a man who knew how to love, and I wasn’t a woman who knew how to either. Yet if I had the chance to fall again, I’d fall with him forever.<br /><br />Even if we were destined to crash against solid ground.</span>

  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491900657i/22458812._SX540_.png' alt=' photo Add heading_zpspm9knukr.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I know I say this after reading every B Cherry book, but I seriously think THIS book is my favorite of hers. Brittainy- <br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Every word you’ve ever written becomes my new favorite story.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b>  Lucy and Graham’s story is original, beautiful, and completely unforgettable! <br/><br/><i>The Gravity of Us</i> starts with Lucille Palmer. A heroine with loads of strength, love, and the biggest heart. Lucy has 2 older sisters and they all lost their free spirited mama years ago. Out of </span>
  <span id="freeText687345442593685311" style="display:none"><b>5+ Graham Cracker stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/Add%20heading_zpspm9knukr.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491900657i/22458812._SX540_.png" alt=" photo Add heading_zpspm9knukr.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I know I say this after reading every B Cherry book, but I seriously think THIS book is my favorite of hers. Brittainy- <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Every word you’ve ever written becomes my new favorite story.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b>  Lucy and Graham’s story is original, beautiful, and completely unforgettable! <br><br><i>The Gravity of Us</i> starts with Lucille Palmer. A heroine with loads of strength, love, and the biggest heart. Lucy has 2 older sisters and they all lost their free spirited mama years ago. Out of all the girls, Lucy is the one most like her mama. She’s sort of a ‘hippie weirdo’ and I mean that in the best possible way. Lucy is one of the best heroines I’ve ever read about and by far my favorite character Brittainy Cherry has ever written. I loved every single thing about her. And her nickname for Graham- best thing ever!!!<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Lucille—”<br>“You can call me Lucy.” <br>“How old are you?”<br>“Twenty-six.” <br>“Lucy is a name for a child. If you ever truly want to make it in the world, you should go by Lucille.” <br>“Noted. If you ever want to be the life of the party, you should consider the nickname Graham Cracker.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/Add%20heading-2_zpswepkk9md.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491900657i/22458813._SX540_.png" alt=" photo Add heading-2_zpswepkk9md.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lucy and Graham meet under interesting circumstances. It’s safe to say that they are opposites. Lucy is fun, free, and happy, where as Graham is taciturn, grounded, and grouchy. This is a story of opposites who are thrown together and some how, some way fall for each other. At first, Lucy drives Graham crazy, but with time, she grows on him. In fact, she is one of the very few people in this world Graham can stand. I loved how different they were from one another. Seeing the way Graham changed and evolved afters spending time with Lucy was one of my favorite parts of the story. I love how one person can come into your life and change everything for you. <br><i>
  <blockquote>I wanted to know what it meant to be a part of her world. To be a man who felt everything.</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/Add%20heading-3_zpslspxcot9.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491900657i/22458814._SX540_.png" alt=" photo Add heading-3_zpslspxcot9.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don’t want to delve too deep into the story. I loved all the moments that made me gasp and watching how everything came together. Just know this story is exceptional. It’s a forbidden(ish) love story, but it’s also a journey. These characters go through a lot but everything that happens happens for a reason (MAKTUB). Not only did I adore Lucy and Graham, but there were some exceptional supporting characters. Ollie was by far my favorite. <br><br>Brittainy’s writing is stunning. It’s epic and brilliant and just everything. Her stories are unlike any authors out there. Every book she writes is unique and emotional and she knows just how to get me in the feels. Every book Brittainy writes makes its way onto my favorites list. She’s that kind of author. Her books are truly special and one of a kind. So many of her quotes speak to me and I just can’t get enough! <i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Sometimes when your heart wanted a full-length novel, the world only gave you a novella, and sometimes when you wanted forever you only had those few seconds of now. And all I could do, all anyone could ever do, was make each moment count.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><i>The Gravity of Us</i> pulled me in from the very first page and never let go. It moved me, made me think, made me feel, and made me fall in love. I laughed, I cried, I cried some more, but I was left with a full heart and a huge smile on my face when I was finished reading. This book is going on my all time favorites book and is my top read of 2017 so far! I give it 5+ stars and recommend it to everyone!! <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Love doesn’t push things away. Love doesn’t suffocate. It makes the world bloom. She taught me that. She taught me how love works.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/Add%20heading-4_zpsrjrryrs4.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491900657i/22458815._SX540_.png" alt=" photo Add heading-4_zpsrjrryrs4.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>beta copy provided by author</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="687345442593685311" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1954376925" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1954376925" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1954376925?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1954376925" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5099637155497835495"><i>
  <b>"I’d died a million deaths before I gave living a chance, and my first breath of life was taken from her lips."</b>
</i><br/><br/>I swear, every time I read this author, I AM WOW'ED. To the point that I have NO IDEA what to say in a review. In fact, I don't think I've ever managed to finish a review on one of Brittainy Cherry's books because all I have is <i>"OMG! OMFG! OMG! OMG! OMGGGG! OMG!"</i> at the end! She leaves me speechless. <br/><br/><b>EVERY. SINGLE. TIME.</b> It never ever ever fails. I'm left <b>OPEN MOUTHED AND SPEECHLESS</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5099637155497835495" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"I’d died a million deaths before I gave living a chance, and my first breath of life was taken from her lips."</b>
</i><br /><br />I swear, every time I read this author, I AM WOW'ED. To the point that I have NO IDEA what to say in a review. In fact, I don't think I've ever managed to finish a review on one of Brittainy Cherry's books because all I have is <i>"OMG! OMFG! OMG! OMG! OMGGGG! OMG!"</i> at the end! She leaves me speechless. <br /><br /><b>EVERY. SINGLE. TIME.</b> It never ever ever fails. I'm left <b>OPEN MOUTHED AND SPEECHLESS.</b><br /><br />And so, here I sit <b>AGAIN,</b> staring at my blinking cursor, wondering to say to do this justice. And honestly, there's nothing. This is a <b>WOW, WHOA, OMG, ANOTHER LEVEL,</b> kind of book and Brittainy has me in awe! <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"If love were a person, it would be her."</b>
</i><br /><br />I'm going to give you 3 reasons you need this book in YOUR LIFE.<br /><br /><b>1.</b> Brittainy Cherry is a brilliant writer. The kind of writer that makes you close your eyes and just breathe out wow's! It's poetic and beautiful. Some of her lines, her paragraphs, kick you straight in the gut. You can't do anything but sit stunned by the beauty and depth of what she's penned. I think she's one of the BEST indie authors I've ever read. She's original with her content, and I get the sense that she thinks long and tirelessly over EVERY word she allows on her pages. Everything has a meaning. There's no bullshit fluff in her work. She's trying to SHOW her readers something. She's trying to inspire them and that BURNS bright in her novels. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"She was the one thing off-limits, and the only thing I’d ever craved."</b>
</i><br /><br /><b>2.</b> The characters in <i>The Gravity of Us</i> literally stop you in your tracks. They're relatable, heartbreaking, and you fall in love with them fast and hard. Lucy's a free spirit that feels everything in the deepest of ways. When she laughs, she laughs hard. When she loves, she loves fully and unconditionally. And when she hurts, she feels it all over. She's emotional and quirky, dramatic and sweet. A loyal, fierce, and an inspiring female force in this novel.<br /><br />And then we have Graham. Graham who's completely broken. Where Lucy feels it all, Graham feels nothing AT ALL. He lacks empathy, kindness, and isn't afraid to cut you with his words. He's hard to love. Hard to forgive. And he doesn't care about what you think or feel. He's just cruel and mean, yet under all the ugly is a soft, broken spirit just begging to be found and healed. <br /><br />Lucy and Graham are complete opposites. And the way the come to meet and then build a friendship is both inspiring and breathtaking! You will love the slow burn in this. The angst that builds slowly over time it makes you feel like you could burst. The love that slowly builds between Graham and Lucy is pure and right, romantic and once again, BREATHTAKING. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Being around you does something strange to me, something that hasn’t happened in such a long time.” <br />"What happens?” <br />He took my hand in his then led it to his chest, and his next words came out as a whisper. “My heart begins to beat again.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><b>3.</b> The premise of this novel, the way it's written, the flow, the pacing. It's all so well done. <br /><br />Original. <br />Creative. <br />Heart stopping. <br /><br />It's a story line that will keep you hooked from start to finish. It's a little forbidden, but it's not tawdry or overdone. It's not illicit or naughty. It's pure and written so right. This book isn't a forbidden romance just to be a forbidden romance. Everything has meaning, purpose, to the overall story arc. Also, the twists and turns leave you on the edge of your seat. There's are things I just never saw coming. Things that broke me but made this story, oh, so damn good! I truly believe it's one of the most well plotted and thought out novels.<br /><br />Overall, I'm enamored by this author and her way of telling a story. Graham and Lucy are destined and the way fate brings them into each other's lives is absolutely magnificent! I'm in love with the purity of these characters and the message of this novel. I think it's a powerful story of letting love in, letting it shine, allowing yourself to feel the highs and low's even if you're scared. <br /><br />Embrace your fears. <br /><br />We all have a path that is written for us. A path that might contain love and should always contain happiness. We deserve good things. And sometimes, even when dealt the shittiest hand, it's up to YOU to make your situation good. Individual happiness lies within, no matter the situation! <br /><br />I really think this is a <b>MUST READ</b> novel. A 5 star, <b>EPIC, UNFORGETTABLE</b> ride that stole my breath! <b>READ IT.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="5099637155497835495" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer9119525506239526094">~*~The Gravity of Us Official Synopsis~*~<br/>Book Four in The Elements Series<br/>Coming Spring 2017<br/>~*~<br/><br/>Graham Russell and I weren’t made for one another.<br/><br/>I was driven by emotion; he was apathetic. I dreamed while he lived in nightmares. I cried when he had no tears to shed.<br/><br/>Despite his frozen heart and my readiness to run, we sometimes shared seconds. Seconds when our eyes locked and we saw each other’s secrets. Seconds when his lips tasted my fears, and I breathed in his pains. Seconds when we both imagin</span>
  <span id="freeText9119525506239526094" style="display:none">~*~The Gravity of Us Official Synopsis~*~<br />Book Four in The Elements Series<br />Coming Spring 2017<br />~*~<br /><br />Graham Russell and I weren’t made for one another.<br /><br />I was driven by emotion; he was apathetic. I dreamed while he lived in nightmares. I cried when he had no tears to shed.<br /><br />Despite his frozen heart and my readiness to run, we sometimes shared seconds. Seconds when our eyes locked and we saw each other’s secrets. Seconds when his lips tasted my fears, and I breathed in his pains. Seconds when we both imagined what it would be like to love one another.<br /><br />Those seconds left us floating, but when reality knocked us sideways, gravity forced us to descend.<br /><br />Graham Russell wasn’t a man who knew how to love, and I wasn’t a woman who knew how to either. Yet if I had the chance to fall again, I’d fall with him forever.<br /><br />Even if we were destined to crash against solid ground.<br /><br />~*~<br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1813386733?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1813386733" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11726431120789675661"><b> 5 ‘MAKTUB’ STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491763240i/22444145._SY540_.jpg' width='430' height='430' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Brittainy C. Cherry delivers a very unique storyline. This story centers around one of three sisters who were raised differently than the 'norm' with a special spirited mother. Lucy finds herself in the midst of her older sister’s personal life and in turn she steps in and helps out a heartless hero.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>”She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491763240ra/22444148.gif' width='430' height='150' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lucy is an extraordinary heroine. She embodies all the good in the world yet comes across light </span>
  <span id="freeText11726431120789675661" style="display:none"><b> 5 ‘MAKTUB’ STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491763240i/22444145._SY540_.jpg" width="430" height="430" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brittainy C. Cherry delivers a very unique storyline. This story centers around one of three sisters who were raised differently than the 'norm' with a special spirited mother. Lucy finds herself in the midst of her older sister’s personal life and in turn she steps in and helps out a heartless hero.<br><br><b>
  <i>”She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491763240ra/22444148.gif" width="430" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lucy is an extraordinary heroine. She embodies all the good in the world yet comes across light and airy. She is a strong contrast to Graham Russell. Graham is an author who has been hurt and has enormous walls up. In a time of crisis he finds that he needs Lucy’s help and in return a slow burn, forbidden-ish, love story develops.<br><br><b>
  <i>” Her emotions weren’t what made her weak. They were her strength.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491763240ra/22444150.gif" width="430" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The supporting characters to this story were unforgettable as was the love the sisters’ mother gave them all and that they all carry with them each every day. Graham’s transformation and fall for Lucy was so well written it was truly heartfelt and believable. This was a solid story and quite beautiful novel! <br><br><b>
  <i>”Live each day as if it’s the final page. Breathe each moment as if it’s the final word.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491763240ra/22444151.gif" width="430" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>**ARC provided in exchange for an honest review**</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4828638867642008277"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Phew! For a minute I thought this would be another DNF. When a book starts with <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[cancer <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and you start crying on page 7? <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492196997ra/22492910.gif' width='400"/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I gave myself five chapters <i>max</i> before I called it a day.   <span id="freeText4828638867642008277" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br><br>Phew! For a minute I thought this would be another DNF. When a book starts with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[cancer <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and you start crying on page 7? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492196997ra/22492910.gif" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I gave myself five chapters <i>max</i> before I called it a day. I am SO glad I didn’t give up. Because after that bumpy start, I was quickly won over by this beautiful, poignant book and its amazing characters: a girl who feels everything and a man who feels nothing at all.<br><br>I was totally consumed and absorbed by their story. Ms. Cherry once again proved that she is a true master of words. She writes with beauty and simplicity yet profound perception about the human nature. Her style is poetic and lyrical. <br><br>And therein lies my dilemma. You see, I am not a big fan of poetic writing or overly sentimental stories. Not everybody can pull it off. And for me, this book is bordering on being too poetic and overly sentimental. The characters felt too black and white and the dialogue too idealistic and perfect at times. But I couldn't <i>not</i> love it. <br><br>If you love emotional books, don’t pass on this one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510504825i/24426022._SX540_.jpg" width='400"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_2032876021" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2032876021" />
    <a title="Danielle ❤️ Pretty Mess Reading ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44553133-danielle-pretty-mess-reading"><img alt="Danielle ❤️ Pretty Mess Reading ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1476328280p2/44553133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2032876021?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Danielle ❤️ Pretty Mess Reading ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Danielle ❤️ Pretty Mess Reading ❤️" href="/user/show/44553133-danielle-pretty-mess-reading">Danielle ❤️ Pretty Mess Reading ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2032876021" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13351030759201222796"><b>***3 STARS***</b><br/><br/>Unfiltered review here... <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://prettymessreading.wordpress.com/2017/06/19/the-gravity-of-us-by-brittainy-c-cherry/'>https://prettymessreading.wordpress.c...</a><br/>Why did I give this book 3 STARS? Simple. It doesn’t compare to the books I’ve given 4 STARS to. I felt as though I would have been disrespectful to all of my 4 STAR reads if I had shared the same rating between this one and the other 4 STARS.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497921336i/23069636._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I’m going to start with Lucy. I liked her, she was a sweetheart and I could see myself liking her in real life. She makes no apologies for who she is and loves herself enough to </span>
  <span id="freeText13351030759201222796" style="display:none"><b>***3 STARS***</b><br><br>Unfiltered review here... <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://prettymessreading.wordpress.com/2017/06/19/the-gravity-of-us-by-brittainy-c-cherry/">https://prettymessreading.wordpress.c...</a><br>Why did I give this book 3 STARS? Simple. It doesn’t compare to the books I’ve given 4 STARS to. I felt as though I would have been disrespectful to all of my 4 STAR reads if I had shared the same rating between this one and the other 4 STARS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497921336i/23069636._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m going to start with Lucy. I liked her, she was a sweetheart and I could see myself liking her in real life. She makes no apologies for who she is and loves herself enough to not give a damn of what someone thinks of her. She cares about everyone and everything with her whole heart. She even sympathizes with a man she doesn’t even know, who has just lost their father.<br><br>Graham was a cold-hearted man who gave zero fucks about it – my kind of guy. But he was also boring as hell – not my kind of guy. He didn’t have one single fun or entertaining moment in the whole book. All he did was mope around and feel sorry for himself. The boy had daddy issues, which I get but damn, he was putting me to sleep.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497921336i/23069637._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Graham is a best-selling author whose real life was more of a blank page. He had nothing he truly cared about and nothing that he wanted. His only friend was a 70 year old something man.<br><br>Lucy was a florist who’s desire was to spend her warmth and joy with the world. She wanted nothing more than to find a way to help Graham enjoy life and not spend it locked away in his mansion where he could block everything and everyone out.<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all.” – Graham</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>I love myself a good alpha man with a cold heart that a good woman can work her way into but Graham was like a walking black cloud.<br><br>The man was just a walking ad for Prozac. And I like Prozac BTW. It’s helped many lead more productive lives. I just wanted to shove them down Graham’s throat to help him too. Because all in all, he wasn’t a bad person.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497921336i/23069638._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book doesn't take a lot of effort to figure out so I’m not giving anything away when I say they eventually find themselves together and live happily-ever-after. It just sucked that the only other emotional I felt throughout the book was depression. I don’t think I smiled once.<br><br>Per the title of the book, Graham and Lucy are pulled together by gravity, or so the story tries to tell us. I didn’t really see it as such. I felt like they were brought together by circumstance, just like any other relationship. That’s like saying gravity pulled my husband and I together instead of strippers and tequila. But it was a good try and I’m giving this book an A for effort.<br><br><b>Is it a horrible book? </b> <i>No.</i><br><b>Would I recommend this book?</b> <i> It depends on the person. To my sister, no! She hates super sensitive books.</i><br><b>Am I glad I read it?</b> <i>I wouldn’t say I’m glad but I’m not upset about it.</i><br><b>Do you think the author is talented?</b> <i>Yes, I do.</i><br><b>Would I read this book again?</b> <i>Hell, no!</i><br><b>Will I read more books by Brittainy Cherry?</b> <i>If I have nothing better to do, sure.</i><br><br>This book was like listening to Sam Smith and Adele singing everything depressing and wanting Bruno Mars to break in at some point to make you smile again.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>Stalk all things messy...</i>
</b> <br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/prettymessreading/">https://www.instagram.com/prettymessr...</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/prettymessreading/">https://www.facebook.com/prettymessre...</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/prettymessread">https://twitter.com/prettymessread</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13351030759201222796" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1775283087?book_show_action=true">Apr 14, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hulya Kara Yuksel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hulya Kara Yuksel" href="/user/show/32793174-hulya-kara-yuksel">Hulya Kara Yuksel</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1775283087" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5294384662783343071"><i>
  <b>"Loving Lucy Hope Palmer wasn’t a choice; it was my destiny." </b>
</i><br/><br/>Oh Graham, I love you so much. <3<br/><br/>This was my 4th book of Ms.Cherry's and with each book this woman amaze me and left me speechless with her talent. I’m in love with each words of this book, I’m in love Graham & Lucy and I highly recommend to you Elements series. This series are must read… You must read Ms.Cherry’s beautiful words. Trust me, they’re all gonna touch your heart & soul. <3 <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437482947ra/15588641.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/></span>
  <span id="freeText5294384662783343071" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"Loving Lucy Hope Palmer wasn’t a choice; it was my destiny." </b>
</i><br><br>Oh Graham, I love you so much. &lt;3<br><br>This was my 4th book of Ms.Cherry's and with each book this woman amaze me and left me speechless with her talent. I’m in love with each words of this book, I’m in love Graham &amp; Lucy and I highly recommend to you Elements series. This series are must read… You must read Ms.Cherry’s beautiful words. Trust me, they’re all gonna touch your heart &amp; soul. &lt;3 <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437482947ra/15588641.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1776366987" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1776366987" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1776366987?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=pure-perfection">pure-perfection</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=top-fantasy-boyfriends">top-fantasy-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=books-that-deserve-more-than-five-s">books-that-deserve-more-than-five-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=best-of-2017">best-of-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=amazing">amazing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=breathtaking">breathtaking</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1776366987" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6986859517074477080"><b>*****FIVE BAZILLION STARS*****</b><br/>{ARC Generously Provided by Author}<br/><br/><br/><b>Right after we soared to our highest heights, we descended and crashed to our lowest lows—but not before his air became my breaths, not before his earth became my ground. His flames were my fire, his thirst was my water, and his spirit?<br/><br/>His spirit became my soul.<br/>Then, we prepared ourselves for goodbye.</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/SBPR-BCC-TGOU-Teaser3_zpszsdbtm9n.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492981805i/22573305._SX540_.png' alt=' photo SBPR-BCC-TGOU-Teaser3_zpszsdbtm9n.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>If you're looking for perfection, this book right here is it!!!<br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>After having read several of Brittainy Cherry’s books, I am convin</span>
  <span id="freeText6986859517074477080" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE BAZILLION STARS*****</b><br>{ARC Generously Provided by Author}<br><br><br><b>Right after we soared to our highest heights, we descended and crashed to our lowest lows—but not before his air became my breaths, not before his earth became my ground. His flames were my fire, his thirst was my water, and his spirit?<br><br>His spirit became my soul.<br>Then, we prepared ourselves for goodbye.</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/SBPR-BCC-TGOU-Teaser3_zpszsdbtm9n.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492981805i/22573305._SX540_.png" alt=" photo SBPR-BCC-TGOU-Teaser3_zpszsdbtm9n.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>If you're looking for perfection, this book right here is it!!!<br><br><br><br><br>After having read several of Brittainy Cherry’s books, I am convinced that she is currently one of the greatest writers out there! Her words come together to create some of the most heart-achingly beautiful characters and stories. I am not even sure that I could come up with a review worthy enough to express just how much this story affected me! All I can say is that this might possibly be my favorite installment in the <i>
  <b>Elements</b>
</i> series. The author truly saved the best for last. I doubt anyone who picks up this book will not fall madly in love with the utter beauty that lays within these pages.<br><br><br><br>Lucy Palmer is the youngest of three sisters and out of the three, she is the one who is most like their mother. Her mom was a free spirit, always on the move and nearly broke for most of their lives. She never gave her daughters financial stability but she more than made up for it with her unequivocal love that she had for them. Before her mother dies, she asks Lucy to take care of her sisters because she knew out of the three sisters, Lucy was the one with the biggest heart which had the capacity to love deeper than her two siblings. Their mother’s death strengthens the bond between Lucy and her sister, Mari but, their oldest sister, Lyric, ends up walking out on her family to build a life for herself.<br><br><br><br>Years later Lyric comes back into Lucy’s life but it’s not under the best of circumstances. Lyric, ‘aka’ Jane, is now a lawyer and married to a very successful but abrasive best-selling author of horror. She’s just given birth to a baby girl, who is almost three months premature. In a state of panic and because Jane does not have a maternal bone in her body, she ends up abandoning her husband and child without a backward glance. And Lucy, being the beautiful person that she is, comes to the aid of her sister’s overwhelmed and socially inept brother-in-law, Graham Russell.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/SBPR-BCC-TGOU-Teaser5_zps5whwol1x.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492981805i/22573306._SX540_.png" alt=" photo SBPR-BCC-TGOU-Teaser5_zps5whwol1x.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>At first, the relationship between Graham and Lucy is beyond awkward and strained. Graham is a very prickly man and not at all easy to be around. Once the story unfolds and the many layers are peeled away from his course exterior, we get to see what made this man turn as cold as ice. What’s even more beautiful is just how much capacity Graham’s heart has to offer undying love. He eventually sees what so many others took for granted in Lucy and all he wants is to shower her with the love she has always been searching for.<br><br><br><br>At first, it will be hard to fathom how Graham and Lucy can ever end up together because of his marriage to her sister and the fact that Lucy has a boyfriend. I will say this, I never for once felt that “cheating” was ever an issue in this story. They didn’t jump into anything lightly and there was definitely a slow and tender build to the romance, and yet never did I feel like things needed to happen sooner, and there wasn’t one single moment that I wasn’t absolutely captivated by this story. <br><br><br><br><b>THE GRAVITY OF US</b> is currently available! Make sure you get to this one asap! This is one of those books that will leave an indelible effect on your soul.<br><br><br><br>Amazon US: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2ok3xtx">http://amzn.to/2ok3xtx</a><br>Amazon UK: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/HfzJ5h">https://goo.gl/HfzJ5h</a><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/14160636_zpsskp0scnk.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489934277ra/22264129.gif" alt=" photo 14160636_zpsskp0scnk.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452041283i/17638294.png" alt=" photo 17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</span>
  <a data-text-id="6986859517074477080" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</a><br/><br/><i>
  <b> For an author, he was unnervingly good-looking and fit. A tattoo traveled up his left arm, wrapping around to the back of his shoulder blade, and his arms appeared as if his biceps had their own biceps, who had then given birth to their own biceps. <br/>For a moment, I considered if he truly was an author and not Dwayne Johnson. </b>

  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491694853ra/22437593.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Each book within the series is a standalone so they don't have to be read in any particular order. What I loved the most about this book was the </span>
  <span id="freeText13190520106975923704" style="display:none"><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=x0y9dw" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=116uwcz" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=30nc3fp" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><i>
  <b> For an author, he was unnervingly good-looking and fit. A tattoo traveled up his left arm, wrapping around to the back of his shoulder blade, and his arms appeared as if his biceps had their own biceps, who had then given birth to their own biceps. <br>For a moment, I considered if he truly was an author and not Dwayne Johnson. </b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=nx8g77" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491694853ra/22437593.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Each book within the series is a standalone so they don't have to be read in any particular order. What I loved the most about this book was the simplicity of the story, this author created such a life like storyline which made it so much more believable and allowed for a deeper connection not only with the written words but with the characters themselves.<br><br><b> She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all. </b><br><br>An unconventional meeting sees Lucy meeting the elusive author in a back alley where they are both locked out of an event centre where her floral business ‘Monet’s Gardens’ catered for Graham's funeral of his estranged father.<br><br>But when that door finally sprigs open it has a domino effect and Graham is calling on Lucy to help him. <br><br><i> “ Words freed me from falling too deep into my mind where I stored all the pain from my past. Without writing, my world would be filled with loss. Without words, I’d be shattered.” </i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=20qhlck" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491770811i/22444757._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>While Lucille is a positive love life to the fullest outgoing kind of person. Graham is a moody, complex closed off to all aspects of life kind of man, to open up is to feel. A dysfunctional up bringing has bearing on the man he is today. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=28it5d2" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491770811ra/22444758.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> “ You’re both hot and cold all at once, and I cannot for the life of me figure you out. I don’t know how to read you, Graham Russell. I pride myself on being able to read people, but you are different.” </i><br><br>There is no better feeling in the world than to pick up a book and to find yourself transported to a world of feels. And ‘The Gravity of Us’ delivers that tenfold.<br>Wow, what an epic journey.<br><br>The Gravity of Us: A slow burn Romantic story by Brittainy C. Cherry is the fourth book in (Elements, #4) Series. The Gravity of Us is told in a dual POV’S. Meet Lucy and Graham. <br>These two characters are complete polar opposites of one another. He’s the closed off broody non feeling author and she’s the hippy weirdo woman that wears her heart on her sleeve and feels everything.<br><br>Thank you for the opportunity to review this book I can't wait to read more from this author.</span>

I'd died a million deaths before I gave living a chance, and my first</i></span>
  <span id="freeText12351239821303583457" style="display:none"><b>I think my eyes hurt from rolling so much at the purple prose.</b> Here are some examples that had me dying a little inside:<br /><br />The mantra of one of the main characters:<br /><i>"Air above me, earth below me, fire within me, water surround me, spirit becomes me."</i><br /><br />The description of their first kiss AS IT WAS HAPPENING:<br /><i>"I felt her entire being wrapping around my soul, soaking me in, changing me into a better man than I'd ever thought I could be. I'd died a million deaths before I gave living a chance, and my first breath of life was taken from her lips."</i><br /><br />A description of them having sex for the first time:<br /><i>"He kissed me with his always, and I kissed him with my forever. Right after we soared to our highest heights, we descended and crashed to our lowest lows-but not before his air became my breaths, not before his earth became my ground. His flames were my fire, his thirst was my water, and his spirit? His spirit became my soul."</i><br /><br />I mean, seriously. Stop it. STOP. IT.<br /><br />Also, I am obviously still very much in a book reading slump. I mean, this book has an average rating of 4.43 and my friends average rating was 4.12 and I still kind of hated this book! :( <br /><br />I'll try to attempt an actual review this time:<br />Lucy - the heroine who annoyed the heck out of me. She spouts the random crap about earth/fire/water/spirit in order to fit the "hippy" label that the author tries to give her. Oh and she likes trees/flowers/gardening, because of course. Also, she is a doormat.<br /><br />Graham - the hero who is an absolute ass and got married for unknown reasons which completely does not fit everything else about him. Also, he magically changes with his love for another woman. <b>Also, can I just say that the name Talon for a girl is absolutely terrible? </b></span>

<div id="review_1865824936" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1865824936" />
    <a title="Sabrina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18085807-sabrina"><img alt="Sabrina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1392065462p2/18085807.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1865824936?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sabrina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sabrina" href="/user/show/18085807-sabrina">Sabrina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=arc-edelweiss-netgalley">arc-edelweiss-netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1865824936" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3367704030791366554"><b>NOW LIVE!!!</b><br/>*<a href='http://amzn.to/2phm4HA' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a>*<a href='http://amzn.to/2oVEIp6' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a>*<br/><br/>Brittainy C. Cherry has never failed to make me cry my eyes out so I really don't know why the emotions this book made me feel came as such a surprise. Maybe because they hit me in an almost sneaky kind of way. When we're introduced to Lucy and Graham we got humor, and intrigue more than anything else. Seeing how different their personalities were sucked me right in and I couldn't help but laugh at Graham when he seemed to just not understand the concept of happin</span>
  <span id="freeText3367704030791366554" style="display:none"><b>NOW LIVE!!!</b><br />*<a href="http://amzn.to/2phm4HA" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a>*<a href="http://amzn.to/2oVEIp6" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a>*<br /><br />Brittainy C. Cherry has never failed to make me cry my eyes out so I really don't know why the emotions this book made me feel came as such a surprise. Maybe because they hit me in an almost sneaky kind of way. When we're introduced to Lucy and Graham we got humor, and intrigue more than anything else. Seeing how different their personalities were sucked me right in and I couldn't help but laugh at Graham when he seemed to just not understand the concept of happiness. <br /><br />And then <b>BAM</b> the sadness and the pain came at me and ruined my soul. I honestly don't think I stopped crying the entire last 30% of this book and it was the best feeling to experience. Yes that sounds crazy, but this was sadness that makes you cry all while being deliriously happy when those tears turn from pain to happiness. <br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Live each day as if it’s the final page. Breathe each moment as if it’s the final word."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />I connected to these characters instantly and fell for them really hard. Lucy was this fun and bubbly type of character that I adored getting to read about. Usually I'm not a lover of the super positive heroines that never see the bad in life. But with Lucy she saw the bad, and then turned it into something great, and I loved seeing that.<br /><br />Graham was so different than her but his character had a lot of depth and once you actually dug into that it was brilliant. I really liked how complex he was and that he came off as this unfeeling bastard, when really he felt just as much as Lucy did. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Bottom line, this is a book I will recommend for everyone. It was truly amazing and I think it will hit peoples emotions the way it did mine, which will make you love it. <br /><i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1948988652" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1948988652" />
    <a title="Megan✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog"><img alt="Megan✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514899021p2/25781525.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1948988652?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Megan✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Megan✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" href="/user/show/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog">Megan✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=can-t-wait">can-t-wait</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=beautifully-written">beautifully-written</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=favorite-author">favorite-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=high-expectations">high-expectations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=tortured_hero">tortured_hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1948988652" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11814066301942413013"><b>*****5 Stars*****</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Air above me, earth below me, fire within me, water surround me, spirit becomes me.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492931516i/22567740._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Brittainy C. Cherry has done it again with another outstanding story in her Elements series. <i>‘The Gravity of Us’</i> was absolutely phenomenal and I could not fault it. Some authors I hold in such a high regard, where their books have a profound impact on me in a way that other authors aren’t able to do. Brittainy C. Cherry is one of those authors. Her writing is always so beautiful and easy to </span>
  <span id="freeText11814066301942413013" style="display:none"><b>*****5 Stars*****</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“Air above me, earth below me, fire within me, water surround me, spirit becomes me.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492931516i/22567740._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brittainy C. Cherry has done it again with another outstanding story in her Elements series. <i>‘The Gravity of Us’</i> was absolutely phenomenal and I could not fault it. Some authors I hold in such a high regard, where their books have a profound impact on me in a way that other authors aren’t able to do. Brittainy C. Cherry is one of those authors. Her writing is always so beautiful and easy to read, that I get invested in the story and feel like I’m living it along with these characters, I feel each touch, the heartbreak and the joy of the characters. I am yet to read one of her books that I don’t utterly adore, hence why she is one of my favourite authors. I have never given any of her books less than 5 stars and I don’t think I can say that for any other author I have reviewed. If you haven’t checked out any of her books yet, then do yourself a favour and one-click this author, because you won’t be sorry. <br><br>To date I don’t believe a character in any story I have read has moved me more than Lucille “Lucy” Palmer. She is such a positive ray of sunshine; she constantly wears her heart on her sleeve and always sees the best in everyone and every situation. Lucy is one of three sisters and is the one who is most like her mama, a free-spirted hippie. She loves easily and without condition and feels absolutely everything; from love and happiness to sorrow and despair. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Even the darkest souls can find some kind of light from your smile.”</i>
</b><br><br>Graham is the polar opposite of Lucy; while Lucy is light, Graham is dark. He is a brooding, sullen individual and has made himself numb to any feelings. He has not had an easy life and as a result has built up so many walls around himself, protecting himself from experiencing any more pain again. Not surprising he has a very hard time letting his guard down; to let someone in and become vulnerable is something he avoids. Of course, once he does do this, they will see how truly amazing he really is. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Graham was a monster born from the ugliest of circumstances. He was painfully beautiful in such a dark, tragic way. His words urged me to go while his eyes begged me to stay.”</i>
</b><br><br>Lucy and Graham are brought together through unfortunate circumstances. Lucy being the selfless and loving person she is takes it upon herself to help Graham and as a result, a beautiful slow burn love develops. Lucy doesn’t put up with Graham’s grumpy ways and ultimately mends his broken heart. She teaches him that it’s ok to open your heart to the prospect of love and to move past the risk of more pain and heartache. They really were the perfect couple; they complimented each other and accepted each other for who they were, flaws and all. I’ve never read a story before where two opposites worked so well together. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Lucy Palmer had saved me from the darkness, and I’d never be able to thank her enough.”</i>
</b><br><br>This compelling and beautifully written story had me enthralled from page one. It made me laugh, made me cry and made me fall in love. This story is about love, loss, family, friendship and ultimately finding that one special person who has the power to be the light in your dark world. <i>'The Gravity of Us'</i> was definitely an unforgettable story that moved me beyond recognition and I would recommend this story to anyone who has the appetite for beautifully written words that will stay with you forever.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11814066301942413013" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer4493783714468961539">+5 Awesome Stars <333<br/><br/>"We weren't supposed to fall for one another, she and I.<br/>Yet it seemed gravity had a way of pulling us closer."<br/><br/>Brittainy delivers an unforgettable,beautiful,unique and original story. The Gravity of Us is an emotional,intense and heartbreaking story.I don't know where to start and what to say,because when I finished this book I was speechless.Seriously and now after two days I'm still thinking about this.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491923035i/22462486._SY540_.jpg' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Apart from the story the characters also touched me in so many ways.I co</span>
  <span id="freeText4493783714468961539" style="display:none">+5 Awesome Stars &lt;333<br><br>"We weren't supposed to fall for one another, she and I.<br>Yet it seemed gravity had a way of pulling us closer."<br><br>Brittainy delivers an unforgettable,beautiful,unique and original story. The Gravity of Us is an emotional,intense and heartbreaking story.I don't know where to start and what to say,because when I finished this book I was speechless.Seriously and now after two days I'm still thinking about this.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491923035i/22462486._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Apart from the story the characters also touched me in so many ways.I connected with them and I could feel everything.Lucy is one of my favorite heroines in this series,she is kind,sweet and lovely.<br><br>"This is who I am.I am the girl who feels everything."<br><br>Graham isn't the best hero from the first moment but as you read more about him,you fell in love with him and you want to hold him forever!Lucy and Graham are totally different and it isn't a love at first sight but when it happened they fell hard for each other.<br><br>"When his head rose and our eyes locked, I swore he somehow squeezed my heart with his stare."<br><br>Rest assured that you will not be disappointed with this one!For one more time Brittainy impressed.She is so talented and each one of her books are perfection!<br><br> <a href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472313906i/20179654.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><div>

  <span id="freeText6821378127237045195" style="display:none">Viva-la-Melty!!!!!!!!!!!!! .....<br /><br />THANK YOU *Carol*! <br /><br />Audiobook --read by Erin Mallon, Brian Pallino ......terrific voices!!!! **GREAT AUDIOBOOK**!!!<br /><br />Romance books --romantic comedy -- heartfelt stories about love - relationship complexities --are on the RISE! They are popping up everywhere! (for mainstream literary readers too) <br /><br />Do NOT let this book cover (the hottie with sexy abbs) jade your assumptions! <br />.....Some serious issues are going on in this novel. <br />.....A mother leaves her newborn!<br />.....The newborn was premature. (and very sick for months) <br />.....The father was clueless about babies! (all new parents are -but he 'really' is) --<br /><br /><br />The father- Graham - **is** a stud-gifted -successful author! The guy can write --but he sure can be an ass! yet. We love the guy anyway! Watching him become 'human' is almost painful. haha!<br /><br />I WAS HOOKED HOOKED HOOKED..............loved listening to this Audiobook! <br />GREAT DIALOGUE --all in the name of love and war --haha! <br /><br />Lucy is the girl we love -- How in the world can a person NOT love Lucy? <br /><br />Here's a funny -- (it was suppose to be serious --and it 'is' the truth) --- but I laughed out loud by the way *Graham* said these words: <br /> "She wore her heart on her sleeve, and I wore mine locked up under chains" ----- want to gag? -- laugh? roll your eyes? --- I just laughed!!! cheesy! Pure enjoyment storytelling!!! <br /><br />Graham Crackers take on a whole new meaning!!</span>
