<div id="review_1775287834" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1775287834" />
    <a title="Jeannine Allison" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30604562-jeannine-allison"><img alt="Jeannine Allison" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1488001283p2/30604562.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1775287834?book_show_action=true">Oct 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jeannine Allison" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jeannine Allison" href="/user/show/30604562-jeannine-allison">Jeannine Allison</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=bawling-like-a-baby">bawling-like-a-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=perfect-title">perfect-title</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=love-the-heroine">love-the-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=99c-or-free">99c-or-free</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=swoon">swoon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=signed-paperbacks">signed-paperbacks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=cover-love">cover-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=famous-people">famous-people</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1775287834" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16476377836723713062">4.25 stars...<br/><br/>✓ Finished in a day<br/>✓ Highlighted the crap out of the book<br/>✓ Cried like a hormonal baby<br/><br/>Yup. I definitely just finished a BCC book... I swear to God, this woman's writing pulls me in like nothing else. Even if I have quibbles with the plot, I still tear through her books and enjoy the hell out of them. This is definitely my favorite in the Elements series. I <i>really</i> liked the two main characters, like a lot a lot, and I enjoyed the heck out of the slow burn in their relationship (which </span>
  <span id="freeText16476377836723713062" style="display:none">4.25 stars...<br><br>✓ Finished in a day<br>✓ Highlighted the crap out of the book<br>✓ Cried like a hormonal baby<br><br>Yup. I definitely just finished a BCC book... I swear to God, this woman's writing pulls me in like nothing else. Even if I have quibbles with the plot, I still tear through her books and enjoy the hell out of them. This is definitely my favorite in the Elements series. I <i>really</i> liked the two main characters, like a lot a lot, and I enjoyed the heck out of the slow burn in their relationship (which is pretty rare for me).<br><br><b>- Lucy -</b><br><br>Lucy was a ray of sunshine ☀️ I loved her upbeat and positive personality. There aren't many heroines like her and found her so refreshing. It was also amazing how she never apologized for who she was. She wasn't afraid to be different.<blockquote>
  <i>"Just because I'm not like you doesn't mean I'm weak."</i>
</blockquote>It wasn't always clear to see from her perspective, but I loved the way Graham saw her...<blockquote>
  <i>She was all over the place: flighty, random, passionate, and emotionally overcharged. It was as if she was fully aware of her faults, and she allowed them to exist regardless. Somehow those faults made her whole.</i>
</blockquote>And her sassiness certainly didn't hurt 😉<blockquote>
  <i>One day I'd stop being so nosey, but obviously that day wasn't today.</i>
</blockquote>I know some people might see her as a pushover, but I never did. I think it takes a lot of courage to forgive the way she does. It's not always easy and some people don't deserve it; it's certainly not something I can always relate to (I can be quite petty 🙈), but I love characters like her. Her unapologetic nature was heartwarming and inspiring. She was always there for Graham, no matter what.<blockquote>
  <i>"If you need to fall, fall into me."</i>
</blockquote><b>- Graham -</b><br><br>*le sigh* I had a pretty big girl crush on Lucy, but Graham?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473531888ra/20477899.gif" width="375" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeah. I'm in love 😍😍😍 I'm a sucker for a hero who starts out being a Grinch and ends up having a heart of gold 💛 He's dismissive of Lucy but I never thought he was overly rude, I've certainly read worst characters. Graham was bitter and wanted to be left alone, and it was very obvious...<blockquote>
  <i>"I shouldn't be surprised by humans at all, but still, each day they tend to shock me with their lack of intelligence."</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>"Please excuse me, I must go someplace other than right here," Graham coldly stated.</i>
</blockquote>He didn't know how to handle Lucy's temperament and I think that exacerbated his negative feelings. But he slowly came around and I loved LOVED <b>LOVED</b> the wisdom he had to offer. This quote right is one of my favorite from the book...<blockquote>
  <i>"Just because you smile and act free doesn't mean the cage doesn't exist. It merely means you lowered your standards for how far you'll allow yourself to fly."</i>
</blockquote>Add to this that he's a writer and a doting father...<blockquote>
  <i>Talon was my savior, and I'd promised myself to be a dad to her, not merely a father. Any person could be a father. It took a real man to step up to the role of being a dad. And I owed that to her. She deserved to have me fully.</i>
</blockquote>AND then he gets super swoony?<blockquote>
  <i>"You're a prize of a woman, rose petals in your hair and all."</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>"You make the world a lot less dark."</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>Loving Lucy Hope Palmer wasn't a choice; it was my destiny.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>If love were a person, it would be her.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>"My greatest hope is, and always will be, you."</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>There was something romantic about the way she moved throughout the world, the way she danced on her tiptoes and laughed without any regard for appearing ridiculous. There was something so true about how she held one's eye contact, and the way she smiled.</i>
</blockquote>I was fucking done for.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494886191ra/22762624.gif" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, I know that was a lot of quotes. And no, I don't care. That was the narrowed down list, so consider yourself lucky 😋<br><br><b>- Graham + Lucy -</b><br><br>From the very beginning they had a complicated relationship.<blockquote>
  <i>She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all.</i>
</blockquote>They both recognized their differences, but they couldn't help but be drawn to one another.<blockquote>
  <i>We weren't supposed to fall for one another, she and I. Yet it seemed gravity had a way of pulling us closer.</i>
</blockquote>I didn't fully understand the forbidden aspect of their relationship. Yes, [MAJOR SPOILERS] <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he was "technically" married to her sister, but they were over. Maybe I'm a shitty person or I have low morals, but I'm not a person who gets hung up on technicalities. Jane (his wife) was a horrible person who abandoned him and their newborn daughter (who we later learn wasn't Graham's at all because she'd cheated on him with his father 😖) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>So, no, I didn't feel like their relationship was wrong. I understand their reluctance because it was a tricky situation but I don't think they deserved to feel guilt or that anyone should have given them crap for their feelings. Another thing I loved a lot about Graham was how he stuck to his feelings. There was push and pull in the beginning, but once he committed, he was all in.<blockquote>
  <i>"It's not going to be easy. It might be very hard, and weird, and out of the norm, but I promise you, if you give me a chance, if you give us a few moments, I'll make it worth all of your time. Say okay?"</i>
</blockquote>And can we take a minute to appreciate this amazing quote?<blockquote>
  <i>Our kiss was as if heaven and hell collided together, and each choice was right and wrong at the same exact time. We kissed as if we were making a mistake and the best decision all at once. His lips made me float higher, yet somehow descend. His breaths somehow made my heart beat faster as it came to a complete halt. Our love was everything good and bad wrapped in one kiss.</i>
</blockquote><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1502432794ra/23560547.gif" width="525" height="425" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved so much about this book, but unfortunately, just like the other books, the ending kept this from being 5 stars for me. I haven't loved any of the ending conflicts in this series. They've all felt OTT and a bit forced, in my opinion. This one was a little different though and the change was what made me like this one better than the others.<br><br>[SIGNIFICANT SPOILERS]<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I loved that the conflict didn't really involve the MCs. Graham didn't push Lucy away like the heroes did in the other three. He wanted to fight for her and hang on to her, and I really loved that. Personally I felt like this ending was the least OTT of the four. That being said, I couldn't justify either of Lucy's sisters nor their actions.<br><br>In the beginning I really liked Mari. Even when she took her jerk of a husband back (I didn't like it and I wanted to smack some sense into her, but I kinda got it), I was still rooting for the day that she kicked him to the curb. For obvious reasons (once you read it) I never liked Lyric (Jane), their older sister who ignored them for years. I was set in how I felt about them, but then they did some things that didn't make sense to me. Their personalities seemed to change for the sole purpose of creating the conflict at the end.<br><br><b>- Lyric -</b><br><br>I was glad that Lyric was still a bitch, because I hate when everyone magically loves everyone at the end of books. So I appreciated that consistency. But her appearance at the end makes no sense. She never wanted children and she abandoned her daughter when she was only weeks old. Her words contradicted her actions.<blockquote><i>"You need to let me see her. As her mother, I deserve that much. It's my right."</i></blockquote>Why now does she feel that way? It felt awfully convenient that she suddenly wanted her daughter, and to blackmail Graham into a real relationship, once Lucy had settled into a relationship with Graham. Lyric even says she doesn't "want to be here." I think the fact that this drama wasn't extremely prolonged help me not feel frustrated, but I kept wondering why it even had to be in there in the first place.<br><br><b>- Mari -</b><br><br>This one hurt (and confused me) more than Lyric's behavior. Mari and Lucy were as close as two sisters could get, but for some reason after Lyric (the sister who abandoned her too) and her douche husband (who left her when she was dying of cancer) whisper some words in her ear she's ready to turn on Lucy? She threw hurtful words at Lucy like <i>she</i> was the one who did something wrong.<blockquote><i>"No, you know what's not fair? Holding it over my head every day that you stayed. Reminding me whenever I have any kind of feelings that you were the one who stuck around to help me during the cancer. So, what, am I now forever indebted to you? I can't move on and live my life?"</i></blockquote>Lucy never made Mari feel indebted to her, she was never trying to make herself seem better for staying, she just didn't understand Mari's loyalty to the two people who left her.<br><br>I can't even really be angry or hate Mari for it because it was so out of character. When the conflict resolves, swiftly I might add, she says...<blockquote><i>"You've been the only constant in my life, and I can't believe I hurt you the way I did."</i></blockquote>I really can't either. I sat and thought about it for a few days and no matter what I do, I can't reason that Mari would actually do what she did. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I was still 100% invested and I certainly didn't hate it, but I wish it had felt more authentic.<br><br>Now I know I included a lot of quotes already, but it's BCC so I have to throw in a <s>few</s> lot more...<blockquote>
  <i>Everything in life happened for a reason, happened exactly how it was meant to, no matter how painful it seemed. Some love stories were meant to be forever, and others just for a season.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>Love. The emotion that made people both soar and crash. The feeling that lit humans up and burned their hearts. The beginning and ending of every journey.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>Nothing good ever came from an unexpected letter written in black ink.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>Real life was a mess of words that sometimes worked, and other times didn't. Real life was an array of emotions that hardly made sense. Real life was a first draft novel with scribbles and crossed out sentences, all written in crayon. It wasn't beautiful. It came without warning. It came without ease.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>Because that was the thing about hearts— when you thought they were completely full, you somehow found room to add a little more love.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>"Being with someone you aren't meant to be with out of fear of being alone isn't worth it. I promise you, you'll spend your life being lonelier with him than you would being without him. Love doesn't push things away. Love doesn't suffocate. It makes the world bloom. She taught me that. She taught me how love works, and I'm certain she taught you the same."</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>Sometimes when your heart wanted a full-length novel, the world only gave you a novella, and sometimes when you wanted forever you only had those few seconds of now. And all I could do, all anyone could ever do, was make each moment count.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>"There might be a million reasons why you think it couldn't work, but all you need is one reason why it could. That reason is love."</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>If only the world could feel the way our hearts beat as one, then maybe they wouldn’t be so harsh to judge our connection.</i>
</blockquote><blockquote>
  <i>"Air above me, earth below me, fire within me, water surround me…"</i>
</blockquote>💛💛💛<br><br>GAH! I love this woman's words. I'm sad that the series is over, but I'm very excited for the future journeys BCC will take us on 🤗<br><br>Safety: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Both MCs are seeing people when they meet. Lucy's boyfriend eventually breaks up with her, and Graham ends up being married to, and has a child with, Lucy's sister. The pregnancy wasn't planned and neither of them love each other. It was more a marriage of convenience. She abandons them early in the novel. Graham even says this...<blockquote><i>We were simply roommates who happened to have sex sometimes... At times my wife was the person I hated the most. While we agreed on many things, sometimes the words that left her mouth made me rethink every flow chart we'd ever made.</i></blockquote> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Closure: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I loved the ending! We get a cute jump ahead epilogue six years later :) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_2367163208" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2367163208" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2367163208?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Rachel Reads Ravenously by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2367163208" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer447693041584103700"><b> 4.5 stars </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all.” </i> </b><br/><br/>The Gravity of Us is the story of Lucille and Graham, an optimist and a pessimist. Circumstances throw them together and Graham ends up needing Lucille even if he doesn’t want to admit it. While Lucille drives him crazy, over time she begins to grow on him and a mutual attraction develops.<br/><br/><b> <i> “It’s just funny, isn’t it? How the main characters never know about the adventures they’re about to go on.” </i> </b><br/><br/>I</span>
  <span id="freeText447693041584103700" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 stars </b><br><br><b> <i> “She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all.” </i> </b><br><br>The Gravity of Us is the story of Lucille and Graham, an optimist and a pessimist. Circumstances throw them together and Graham ends up needing Lucille even if he doesn’t want to admit it. While Lucille drives him crazy, over time she begins to grow on him and a mutual attraction develops.<br><br><b> <i> “It’s just funny, isn’t it? How the main characters never know about the adventures they’re about to go on.” </i> </b><br><br>It’s funny because I don’t normally enjoy very sweet books. And this book is so sweet, but it wasn’t cheesy. And I think that’s why I enjoyed it so much, because I was able to enjoy the sweet and it didn’t make me overdose on it. And while this book was sweet, it was also full of FEELS. ALL THE FEELS. Not the angsty feels, but many feels and I enjoyed that very much.<br><br>What stuck for me most and what made this 4.5 was the beautiful story, the beautiful words, and the beautiful characters. No one was perfect, but they were appreciated for who they were. The romance was built on respect and friendship and that made such a strong foundation. A wonderful slowburn romance.<br><br>Amazing book and it didn’t take long to read, so I recommend you carve out some time and read it asap!<br><br><b> <i> “I imagined what it would be like to be happy, and I think you are the definition of happiness.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1965129281" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1965129281" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1965129281?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of evocative romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=family-friendship">family-friendship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=arc-netgalley-request">arc-netgalley-request</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1965129281" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5968342432921064751"><b>Genre: </b> Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b> Standalone Book 4 from Elements series<br/><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491754356i/22443157._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lucille (Lucy) Palmer was a free spirit. She was as bright and lovely as the flowers in her shop. She was never one to shy from embracing her emotions even if it's against a heartless man.<br/><br/>Graham Russell was an award winning fiction author. His books might have heart, but the man himself avoided showing it in real life. That was until she entered his life and showed him what it meant to live </span>
  <span id="freeText5968342432921064751" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b> Standalone Book 4 from Elements series<br><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491754356i/22443157._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lucille (Lucy) Palmer was a free spirit. She was as bright and lovely as the flowers in her shop. She was never one to shy from embracing her emotions even if it's against a heartless man.<br><br>Graham Russell was an award winning fiction author. His books might have heart, but the man himself avoided showing it in real life. That was until she entered his life and showed him what it meant to live a fulfilling life.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I always love books that evoke emotions and I know Brittainy C. Cherry is capable of doing that. This book surely succeeded in that matter.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>If there's one fictional character I could easily relate to, it's Graham. He's cold, apathetic and pretty much an asshole. I feel like I'm the real life reflection of him - except the asshole part (Well, at least I hope not haha!). But behind the facade, he had the capacity to open up his heart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>She was the one thing off-limits, and the only thing I’d ever craved.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Lucy was the complete opposite of Graham. If they were books, he would be a non HEA mystery and she would be a rainbow farting unicorn romance. She brought light and happiness into people's lives without being annoying. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>Heartbreak took love and mutilated it, humiliated it, scarred it. Heartbreak slowly began to freeze heartbeats that had once been so welcoming to love.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I was excited to read this book, but as I progressed, I started to doubt it. I like both characters, but I wasn't "feeling" it. It took close to 70% for it to stir something in me, but as soon as it did, it was an emotional assault, and that's a good thing in my book lol!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>“Being around you does something strange to me, something that hasn’t happened in such a long time.”<br>“What happens?” He took my hand in his then led it to his chest, and his next words came out as a whisper. <br>“My heart begins to beat again.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I like how Graham evolved organically. There's nothing worse when a character flipped like a switch. The writing as usual is beautiful with plenty of quotable sentences.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491754356i/22443158.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Gravity of Us revolves around two individuals who help tether each other to the ground while learning to enjoy the high of life. It would appeal to readers who like to embrace their emotions.<br><br><b>Standalone books in the series:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564446.The_Air_He_Breathes__Elements___1_" title="The Air He Breathes (Elements, #1) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1441375261s/25564446.jpg" alt="The Air He Breathes (Elements, #1) by Brittainy C. Cherry" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26615962.The_Fire_Between_High___Lo__Elements___2_" title="The Fire Between High &amp; Lo (Elements, #2) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1456332708s/26615962.jpg" alt="The Fire Between High &amp; Lo (Elements, #2) by Brittainy C. Cherry" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29963453.The_Silent_Waters__Elements___3_" title="The Silent Waters (Elements, #3) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1472832783s/29963453.jpg" alt="The Silent Waters (Elements, #3) by Brittainy C. Cherry" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/32294951.The_Gravity_of_Us__Elements___4_" title="The Gravity of Us (Elements, #4) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1490620176s/32294951.jpg" alt="The Gravity of Us (Elements, #4) by Brittainy C. Cherry" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454304059i/17942101.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1776662706" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1776662706" />
    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1776662706?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=advanced-copy">advanced-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=abused-in-childhood">abused-in-childhood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=auto-buy-author">auto-buy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=mr-money-bags">mr-money-bags</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=tortured-hero">tortured-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=april2017">april2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1776662706" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10552917700101387403"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396539003i/9148958.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430781822i/14762041.png' width='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Title:</b> The Gravity of Us<br/><b>Series:</b> Elements #4<br/><b>Author:</b> Brittainy C. Cherry<br/><b>Release date: </b> April 13, 2017<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><b>HEA</b><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491952762i/22466453.png' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The Elements series has come to be one of my all time favorite series. I look forward to each book with growing anticipation and excitement, so it's really bittersweet to see this amazing journey come to a close. Graham and Lucy's story was not just a simple straightforward romance from point A to point B. It was more about the exploration of diff</span>
  <span id="freeText10552917700101387403" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396539003i/9148958.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430781822i/14762041.png" width="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Title:</b> The Gravity of Us<br><b>Series:</b> Elements #4<br><b>Author:</b> Brittainy C. Cherry<br><b>Release date: </b> April 13, 2017<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><b>HEA</b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491952762i/22466453.png" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Elements series has come to be one of my all time favorite series. I look forward to each book with growing anticipation and excitement, so it's really bittersweet to see this amazing journey come to a close. Graham and Lucy's story was not just a simple straightforward romance from point A to point B. It was more about the exploration of different types of love, in all the forms and expressions you can experience. The love between blood family. Chosen family. Sisters, fathers, daughters. And how it can make you fly or fall from one breath to the next. This was a slow burn, forbidden romance. And when it all pulled together in the end, it was a thing of beauty. <br><br><b>We weren't supposed to feel this way. We weren't supposed to fall for one another, she and I. Yet it seemed gravity had a way of pulling us together.</b><br><br>Graham Russell is a very emotionally wounded man who learned to shut off his feelings in order to avoid pain. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491924164ra/22462657.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He may have followed in his father's footsteps and become an author, but that's where their relationship ended. His childhood was a minefield of hurt, resentment, and feelings of abandonment by those who ever showed him love. Is it any wonder than the concept of giving love, of showing love became equivalent to weakness? He's just fine writing his bestsellers, closed off from the world, and the foolish people who allow themselves to be vulnerable.<br><br>Lucy Palmer was the complete opposite of Graham. Free spirited, filled with joy and exuberance for life. She gave all of herself, never holding back or concealing how bright she could shine. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491923833ra/22462640.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>When these two come face to face for the first time, it's actually comical how their personalities clash with one another. Surprisingly, though he is extremely rude and cold at the start, there was never a point where I disliked him or got angry at his behavior. Brittainy Cherry knows how to develop characters to make them human. She brings us up close and personal, scars and all. So when we see them thrive and become whole again, it's even more rewarding and precious.<br><br>Seeing Graham slowly soften and express himself with those around him will melt your heart. Lucy showed him how to open himself to the beauty around him and experience the world through her eyes. But he was also her solid ground to stand on when she lost her footing. Together they were balanced and completely in harmony. But there were those who couldn't understand or accept them, and they had to fight to find their forever.<br><br>Yes, I ended up loving this story, just as I have with every book by this author. But for a large portion of the book, I wasn't completely <i>there</i> where I should have been. I almost felt detached, and I can't really pinpoint why to be honest. There was one point where I should have been a sobbing mess and there was nothing. Let me tell you though...the last 25% of the book packs one magnificently powerful blow. It was pure beauty how she tied each piece of the story together. And too see how their love that was planted, grew and flourished to be strong and full of faith. <br><br>My early reticence is most likely entirely on me, so don't let that dissuade you. Brittainy has another winner on her hands, there is no doubt in my mind that everyone will fall for this very unique and special couple. <br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter"               <span id="reviewTextContainer1962847926" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17369517984850228194"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was a total 5 star read for me in the first 80ish%! I felt like the major conflicts were thrown in way too late and resolved way too easily for them to be believable. I am so bummed! I loved this book until then! I knew we had to have the conflict, so I was expecting it...but that late?!? It was accompanied by some other big drama for both the H and h (that felt a little OTT) right at the same time! And all of the conflicts seem to take a complete 180 and turn aro</span>
  <span id="freeText17369517984850228194" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was a total 5 star read for me in the first 80ish%! I felt like the major conflicts were thrown in way too late and resolved way too easily for them to be believable. I am so bummed! I loved this book until then! I knew we had to have the conflict, so I was expecting it...but that late?!? It was accompanied by some other big drama for both the H and h (that felt a little OTT) right at the same time! And all of the conflicts seem to take a complete 180 and turn around without any further issues?!? Yeah...not just bummed -- a little ticked off tbh. <br /><br />Total side note here -- but if all authors had biceps like the H is described to have and that on the cover, I think the ladies are looking for the wrong type of man! ;)<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Lucy and Graham's story. They meet at a funeral where they both get trapped by a locked door. They have an instant pull even though they are total opposites and start talking, and Graham reveals some truths that he hasn't ever done before. Lucy is shocked to find out that Graham is actually married to her estranged older sister. After some traumatic events, Lucy ends up helping Graham out with his new life changing realities. They spend a lot of time together, and help each other through some hard times which only ends up bringing them closer and making the pull harder to ignore. After getting through those hard times, they do get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Lucy and Graham's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good until the last 18ish%. I never skimmed, and I thought it flowed well. <br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No, they take a good while to develop stronger feelings.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Graham. I liked him. He was a bit of an apathetic, but moody guy (if that even makes sense) that said some brutality honest things at times that had to sting -- but I ended up really enjoying his character.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 5 stars. Lucy. I loved her. She was a "hippie weirdo", but I loved that about her! She was always positive, loving, and extremely loyal.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Moderate/high. I needed a few tissues, but it never turned into an ugly cry.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They both want each other, but feel it's wrong because he is married to her sister. The H is the main pursuer of the relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Low. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They have one sex scene in the story. They don't kiss until 78ish% and the scene isn't until 90ish%. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I don't remember any mention of condom use, birth control, std statuses, or previous practices. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ They both are with other people when they meet. The h breaks up with OM, but the H is still technically married when feelings start to develop between them. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> Technically, yes. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H is married to the h's older sister when they meet. The sister leaves him and her daughter, but they are still technically together when feelings for the h start to develop. They kiss and have sex while he is still married to the sister (about a year after she abandoned the baby and the H).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated shortly, but there was no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Loss of a parent (H and h - off page but mentions), Cancer (on page - side character), child abandonment (H's wife - on page), H is married and has child with h's sister (on page), and loss of a parental figure (big side character - on page).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had pretty good closure with a jump ahead epilogue and a HEA ending. See "overall opinion" section above about my issues with the conflicts being resolved too easily.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> It was part of my kindle unlimited subscription.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be either <u>Safe with exception</u> or <u>Not Safe</u> depending on personal preferences.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does</b> have cheating (see above "cheating" spoiler)<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the h pushing the H away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a short (days?) separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts (see above "Trigger" spoiler)<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1956204369" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10880129304065376115"><b>FIVE BILLION STARS *****</b><br/>(BR with Mel <3)<br/><br/>There's not enough beautiful words in the dictionary that could describe this book. Graham and Lucy took me hostage into their vibrant world, where love was able to give color and hope, even to the darkest of hearts. This story made me forget where I was, who I was, and what I was doing; I was only feeling, so many emotions flowing through me at once, I was helpless to the amazing words of this author. <i>The Gravity Of Us</i> is an unforgettable novel that will </span>
  <span id="freeText10880129304065376115" style="display:none"><b>FIVE BILLION STARS *****</b><br>(BR with Mel &lt;3)<br><br>There's not enough beautiful words in the dictionary that could describe this book. Graham and Lucy took me hostage into their vibrant world, where love was able to give color and hope, even to the darkest of hearts. This story made me forget where I was, who I was, and what I was doing; I was only feeling, so many emotions flowing through me at once, I was helpless to the amazing words of this author. <i>The Gravity Of Us</i> is an unforgettable novel that will live on for years in the hearts of its readers. This book has such a meaningful and beautiful message that it could inspire a powerful song, make a wonderful movie, or even be an uplifting poem that can help anyone get through hard times. This book is everything, an absolute must read!!!<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/69823E2D-D926-4B84-90BF-63BF46DB46D4_zpsy8him1m6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491971490i/22467898._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 69823E2D-D926-4B84-90BF-63BF46DB46D4_zpsy8him1m6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lucy and Graham are absolute opposites, where she is light, he is dark, she wears her heart on her sleeve, but he's taught himself not to feel. <br><br>Lucy's mission has been to keep her family together after her mom passed away. Lucy has two sisters whom she adores, even if they sometimes make it hard to love them. Lucy is always looking for the bright side, even in the worst of situations, and she been through enough of those, but she's always ready to face the hard times with a smile. And funny enough, is when Graham is going through a really hard time in his life, when he meets Lucy. <br><br>As much as Graham needs Lucy, AKA "annoying hippie chick" he tries and actually pushes her away a few times. But every time he calls for her, she's there. Lucy's heart is so warm that she ends up thawing Graham's. These two start to form a bond that you just know, right away that will last forever. They learn so much from, and with each other, and the beauty of their relationship is blinding, yet you can't look away. <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/248FA568-ABCA-4835-9360-D60D36A10DF0_zpsp9sra3sx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491971491i/22467899._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 248FA568-ABCA-4835-9360-D60D36A10DF0_zpsp9sra3sx.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If you ever meet author Brittainy Cherry you'll notice how she glows, her beauty and her heart shine so bright so is no wonder you can see that glow shimmering through her stories as well. I've read a lot of her books, and they always blow me away. And just like the rest of her stories, <i>The Gravity Of Us</i> has so much heart and soul inside its pages, and anyone who reads this book will bask in the beauty of this amazing story. <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/CD947C1A-8251-43A0-B6B5-72D4A0A4EE37_zps3rgiutfu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483815159i/21652248._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo CD947C1A-8251-43A0-B6B5-72D4A0A4EE37_zps3rgiutfu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1965151155" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10006766103576104552">reread 1/26/20: same feelings as the first time!<br/><br/><b>the good</b><br/>The best way to describe this book would be like a really sugary glass of tea. Warm & comforting, but also too sweet and not filling. I will say I was honestly amazed at how much i HATED Graham at the start of this, and how quickly the author was able to switch my opinion of him. He is a sweet lil grizzly bear who needs a hug. And I also really liked how Lucy was free spirited yet didn't let people walk all over her. They really were a grea</span>
  <span id="freeText10006766103576104552" style="display:none">reread 1/26/20: same feelings as the first time!<br /><br /><b>the good</b><br />The best way to describe this book would be like a really sugary glass of tea. Warm &amp; comforting, but also too sweet and not filling. I will say I was honestly amazed at how much i HATED Graham at the start of this, and how quickly the author was able to switch my opinion of him. He is a sweet lil grizzly bear who needs a hug. And I also really liked how Lucy was free spirited yet didn't let people walk all over her. They really were a great match, and I love their shared love of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[talon <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br /><b>the bad</b><br />We get flashbacks throughout the story from Graham's childhood but we never see him opening up to Lucy about it or really any sort of communication between them on their pasts. And I don't think this would have bothered me so much if this was the case in the rest of Cherry's books, but it just isn't. She tends to do a pretty good job at keeping her books short <i>and</i> incorporating enough reconciliation of trauma to make her resolutions believable. Additionally, the antagonist of the story is kind of unbelievably horrible but only causes problems for all of 2 seconds. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I'm supposed to believe your dumb ass comes back to see your child after abandoning her &amp; then you're gonna leave like 2 seconds letter? hm. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Overall, I enjoyed this book but it probably won't stick with me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10006766103576104552" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1776831449" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1776831449" />
    <a title="Grecia Robles" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43801560-grecia-robles"><img alt="Grecia Robles" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578037155p2/43801560.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1776831449?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grecia Robles" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grecia Robles" href="/user/show/43801560-grecia-robles">Grecia Robles</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43801560-grecia-robles?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43801560-grecia-robles?shelf=popsugar-2017">popsugar-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43801560-grecia-robles?shelf=5-estrellas">5-estrellas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43801560-grecia-robles?shelf=emocionales">emocionales</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43801560-grecia-robles?shelf=baby-mamma">baby-mamma</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1776831449" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16505907747792279586"><b>****4.999 Todo está escrito STARS****</b><br/><br/><b>
  <u>PopSugar Reading Challenge Categoría #5</u>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I love you, Lucy,” he said, not calling me Lucille for the first time ever. “I love the way you give, the way you care, the way you laugh, the way you smile. I love your heart and how it beats for the world. Before you, I was lost, and because of you, I found my way home. You’re the reason I believe in tomorrow. You’re the reason I believe in love, and I plan to never let you go. Marry me. Marry Talon. Marry</blockquote></i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText16505907747792279586" style="display:none"><b>****4.999 Todo está escrito STARS****</b><br><br><b>
  <u>PopSugar Reading Challenge Categoría #5</u>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I love you, Lucy,” he said, not calling me Lucille for the first time ever. “I love the way you give, the way you care, the way you laugh, the way you smile. I love your heart and how it beats for the world. Before you, I was lost, and because of you, I found my way home. You’re the reason I believe in tomorrow. You’re the reason I believe in love, and I plan to never let you go. Marry me. Marry Talon. Marry us.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Así estoy en estos momentos a segundos de haber terminado este hermoso libro <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381390168ra/4795099.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sé que las altas expectativas son unas perras que te juegan en contra y de verdad que tenía bastante miedo leer este libro tan esperado y que no me gustara pero muy en el fondo de mi corazón sabía que no me iba a decepcionar y no lo hizo, y ahora sí me declaro <b>OFICIALMENTE una fangirl de esta serie</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492330397ra/22505932.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brittainny C. Cherry la volví hacer juro que la volvió hacer, me removió tantas cosas por dentro, con sus escritura tan linda y sus palabras bonitas <s>volví a dejar mi Kindle como un arcoíris</s>, que iban penetrando poco a poquito en mi alma y mi corazón oscuro, hace que conectes con los personajes y que empatices con ellos que sientas sus miedos, fracasos, frustraciones, su dolor y el amor y no fue la excepción con estos protagonistas.<br><br><i> Lucille y Graham dos polos opuestos ella tan libre y el tan encerrado en una jaula, ella vuela y él es la gravedad.</i><br><br>La historia de Lucy y Graham fue bastante linda, sin ese instalove que es tan irreal, oh no ¡! Su amor se fue dando des-pa-sito <s>(se nota que no me traumé con la canción de Luis Fonsi que sale como 100 veces en la radio)</s>, lento de esos amores que disfrutas, que te emocionas con una acción con una mirada y que sin darte cuenta llegas a un punto donde están enamorados y eso es lo que me pasó con Lucy y Graham, además como siempre digo <b>
  <u> No se necesita estar repleto de escenas de sexo para que sea entretenido, es más en este tipo de historias chafa la lectura</u>
</b><br><br>Es una historia dónde el amor es el principal impulsor de todo no sólo de pareja, sino el amor de la familia, de los amigos y el amor que le tiene un padre/madre a un hijo como te cambia la vida y te hace querer ser mejor persona y te cambia la perspectiva de la vida, por ahí hay un dicho popular que dice No es padre el que engendra sino el que cría y es muy cierto y en esta historia no los muestra. Las segundas oportunidades también juegan un papel importante que no es demasiado tarde para darle una oportunidad a la vida.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“After this I need you to go back to being my friend, because being friends with you makes me a better person. You make me a better human.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>Ahora hablemos de los personajes</b><br><br><b>
  <u>Lucille</u>
</b> Que mujer tan más fuerte valiente y buena persona, en serio una gran protagonista de esas que son todo corazón, desinteresadas que dan todo y no piden nada a cambio, ella es un espíritu libre y un alma alegre que con sólo su presencia ilumina la vida de las personas que la rodean <s>Grecia en modo filosófica cursi en su máxima expresión</s>, Lucy es la mejor protagonista de esta serie tenía la valentía que le hizo falta a Maggie May <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>The tears kept falling as she listened to the beautiful vocals, her body rocking slightly as I held her hand. For the first time, I began to understand her fully. The beautiful girl who felt everything. Her emotions weren’t what made her weak.<br>They were her strength</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>”Graham Cracker” </u>
</b> Él es de esos protagonistas que me gustan que son fríos con pasados tormentosos pero que conforme va avanzando la lectura se van derritiendo y derribando sus barreras hasta convertise en unos teddy bears, al principio no veía la manera de enamorarme de él fue un patán bien hecho, pero conforme se fue ablandando soltaba cada frase que me hacía suspirar realmente amé a Graham y en esta serie lo pongo a nivel de Tristán <b>ya que mi amado Brooks está a otro nivel, lo tengo en un pedestal en el cielo., para ti siempre mi corazón </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492330397ra/22505929.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>El libro tuvo sus momentos perfectos y de lloradera <b> STOP !!! Aquí hay Spoilers</b><br> •	Las mejores escenas se las llevó Graham que a pesar de ser un hombre frío que no sentía nada, <br> se convirtió en esos hombres que decían las cosas más lindas del mundo <br><br><i>Loving Lucy Hope Palmer wasn’t a choice; it was my destiny.</i><br><br>•Los momentos con el profesor Ollie, fueron escenas divertidas y conmovedoras y sobre todo su muerte y cuando Graham se desmorona ahí solté mis primeras lágrimas.<br>•Cuando Graham hace el Jardín para Lucy eso fue bello<br>•La propuesta de matrimonio para mí fue PERFECTA, la amé y lo voy admitir mi lado cursi hizo que llorara de felicidad LITERAL lloré <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492330397ra/22505930.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492330528ra/22505944.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ahora que se acabó esta serie no se que va a ser de mí, se convirtió en una de mis series favoritas de la vida, tal vez no sean los mejores libros, puede que tengan drama innecesario que hayas situaciones ilógicas y absurdas PERO a mí me llegó al corazón y tocó fibras sensibles dentro de mí, sobre todo con The Air He Breathes y The Silents Water <b> que este último es mi favorito y él mejor de toda la serie para mi</b>, me identifiqué y los sentí. Esta serie llegó en el momento justo en mi vida donde todavía estaba sufriendo la pérdida de personas queridas tal vez todo está escrito y era el destino que esta serie se cruzara en mi camino <i>Maktub</i><br><br>Con The Air He Breathes aprendí que por muy profunda que sea la pérdida siempre encuentras la luz al final del túnel y el dolor no es para siempre <br>The Silents Waters me enseñó que la vida es de momentos y que hay algunos que nos definen y no hacen las personas que somos por como los afrontamos <br>The Gravity of Us me dejó que la familia no sólo es de sangre, la que comparte tu ADN, sino la que te da amor.<br><br>Me encantó que la autora haya enlazado todas las series con esta frase <br><i>
  <blockquote>Air above me, earth below me, fire within me, water surround me, spirit becomes me</blockquote>
</i><br><br>PD. Me faltaron muchas cosas que poner en esta reseña sobre todo a las personas que odié, pero no merecen mi tiempo y palabras sólo les dejo este mensaje. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492330397ra/22505931.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>PDD: Un dato curioso ¿Se fijaron que todas las protagonistas de esta seire eran rubias?</span>

<div id="review_1963310549" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1963310549" />
    <a title="Wil Loves Books!" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3232198-wil-loves-books"><img alt="Wil Loves Books!" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467223384p2/3232198.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1963310549?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wil Loves Books!" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wil Loves Books!" href="/user/show/3232198-wil-loves-books">Wil Loves Books!</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=on-kindle">on-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=priority-tbr">priority-tbr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=not-yet-released">not-yet-released</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1963310549" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer681280627551059304"><strong>
  <em>“Air above me, earth below me, fire within me, water surround me…” </em>
</strong><br/><br/> <br/><br/>All the stars in the world. This one got me from beginning to end. A-MA-ZING.<br/><br/> <br/><br/>This book! Man, this book simply consumed me. Once I started I had to keep going until I was done. Totally pulled an all-nighter with this one. Brittainy Cherry is simply brilliant. One of the most talented writers there is, definitely one of my favorites. I’m not sure how she does it, but she brings it, every.single.time. When I think one of her b</span>
  <span id="freeText681280627551059304" style="display:none"><strong>
  <em>“Air above me, earth below me, fire within me, water surround me…” </em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br>All the stars in the world. This one got me from beginning to end. A-MA-ZING.<br><br> <br><br>This book! Man, this book simply consumed me. Once I started I had to keep going until I was done. Totally pulled an all-nighter with this one. Brittainy Cherry is simply brilliant. One of the most talented writers there is, definitely one of my favorites. I’m not sure how she does it, but she brings it, every.single.time. When I think one of her books won’t top the last, she wows me over and over again. And well, this one is her latest masterpiece.<br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all.”</em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br>I don’t even know what to say. I want to say a lot and nothing at all. It happens to me every time I read a B. Cherry book. I want to scream at the world “Go! Read This! Now!!!” But I really don’t want to tell you anything else but trust me, you will love this. Sorry, lol. I’m just that speechless after reading this amazing book. I know I say this everything. But this was an EPIC love story, truly epic!<br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em> “You’re both hot and cold all at once, and I cannot for the life of me figure you out. I don’t know how to read you, Graham Russell. I pride myself on being able to read people, but you are different.” </em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em> </em>
</strong><br><br>I guess I still need to give you something, anything. I’ll tell you that this one is all about the characters. The characters are just fantastic, beautiful and amazingly developed. They simply suck you into their story and make you be invested in them. I loved Lucy so much. She was amazing. She’s such a beautiful soul. Amazing free spirit and so full of love. Absolutely loved her!<br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“It was all right that she and I handled things in a different fashion. She wore her heart on her sleeve, and I kept my heart wrapped in steel chains deep within my soul.”</em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br>And Graham, what can I say, beautiful, broken Graham. I have to say I have a super sweet spot for Brittainy’s heroes. They’re always so flawed and often times broken, but they’re also so full of love. And swoony. And gorgeous. In this case, Graham is the opposite of Lucy, harden, closed off, unkind. Yet, there’s so much more about him. By the end, you’ll just love him.<br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“Lucille?” “Yes?” “You make the world a lot less dark.” </em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em> </em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em>We weren’t supposed to feel this way. We weren’t supposed to fall for one another, she and I. Yet it seemed gravity had a way of pulling us closer. </em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em> </em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br>Their relationship is very slow built, it goes from acquaintances, to friends, to lovers. But this definitely makes the story 10 times better, the slow burn, the angst, gahhh, you must read this to figure it out!<br><br> <br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“I couldn’t remember the last time I felt the way I did when I held her hand, or when I saw her caring for Talon, or even when I saw her merely existing.”</em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“Thank you, Graham.” “For what?” “Catching me before I hit the ground.” </em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br>I loved the story. I love that it was different, original, refreshing. I loved how well developed the characters were. I loved the pacing and the slow burn. I loved the romance. And the writing, the brilliant writing. This is without a doubt one of my favorite books this year. All the feels, all the love, all the angst. Simply amazing. I absolutely recommend!!!<br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“Lucille Hope Russell was my love story, and I promised myself I’d spend the rest of my life being hers. After all, maktub—it was already written. We were destined to live happily ever after as our hearts floated near the stars and our feet remained on solid ground.”</em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444752880i/16547832.png" alt="" width="200" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <br><br> <br><br> <br><br>I love soooo many quotes! I’ll just put some of my faves here:<br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>“It’s just funny that it’s happening to you of all people, and you seem one hundred percent ignorant to it.”</em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em> “What are you talking about?” </em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em>“I guess it’s harder to see the plot line when you’re the one living the story.” </em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>Because that was the thing about hearts—when you thought they were completely full, you somehow found room to add a little more love. Loving Lucy Hope Palmer wasn’t a choice; it was my destiny. </em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em> “It’s you,” I whispered, our lips still slightly touching. “My greatest hope is, and always will be, you.” </em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em> </em>
</strong><br><br><strong>
  <em>Sometimes when your heart wanted a full-length novel, the world only gave you a novella, and sometimes when you wanted forever you only had those few seconds of now. And all I could do, all anyone could ever do, was make each moment count. </em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em>If love came with a timeline, Graham Russell would’ve always held my heart. </em>
</strong><br><br> <br><br> <br><br><strong>
  <em> “I love you, Lucy,” he said, not calling me Lucille for the first time ever. “I love the way you give, the way you care, the way you laugh, the way you smile. I love your heart and how it beats for the world. Before you, I was lost, and because of you, I found my way home. You’re the reason I believe in tomorrow. You’re the reason I believe in love, and I plan to never let you go. </em>
</strong><br> <br>**An ARC was generously provided in exchange for an honest review**</span>
