<div id="review_1842372499" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1842372499" />
    <a title=" Sonya ♕Chatterbooks book blog♕" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27885126-sonya-chatterbooks-book-blog"><img alt=" Sonya ♕Chatterbooks book blog♕" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1479013940p2/27885126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1842372499?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Sonya ♕Chatterbooks book blog♕" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Sonya ♕Chatterbooks book blog♕" href="/user/show/27885126-sonya-chatterbooks-book-blog"> Sonya ♕Chatterbooks book blog♕</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34826911-the-gravity-of-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27885126-sonya-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27885126-sonya-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=arcs-2017">arcs-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27885126-sonya-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1842372499" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9298722727599387550">⭐⭐⭐⭐4 Stars ⭐⭐⭐⭐<br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=34p02km' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491235075i/22388498._SX540_.png' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> <i> “Some love stories were meant to be forever, and others just for a season. </i></b>  <br/><br/>I always find myself in awe whenever I read a Brittainy C Cherry book. Her words are poetic and they always become a nurtured balm to my soul. Her ability to tell a story and not only wish you were there in that moment, but to make you FEEL is what reading her stories does to me. Sometimes you think to yourself, how can words touch a person like that? The lyrical sway of each syllable you feel down</span>
  <span id="freeText9298722727599387550" style="display:none">⭐⭐⭐⭐4 Stars ⭐⭐⭐⭐<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=34p02km" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491235075i/22388498._SX540_.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> <i> “Some love stories were meant to be forever, and others just for a season. </i></b>  <br><br>I always find myself in awe whenever I read a Brittainy C Cherry book. Her words are poetic and they always become a nurtured balm to my soul. Her ability to tell a story and not only wish you were there in that moment, but to make you FEEL is what reading her stories does to me. Sometimes you think to yourself, how can words touch a person like that? The lyrical sway of each syllable you feel down to your core and then the moment hits you: Reading this book wasn’t a pleasure. It was an EXPERIENCE.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=35iy7td" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492031573ra/22475464.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lucille Palmer has always wore her heart on her sleeve. She feels every emotion more than others, she cares about people with everything she has, but when she loves? She loves hard. Being known as a free spirit but also the one that can hold her sisters together, Lucille was the type of woman you wanted to have as a friend and as a sister. When she meets her complete opposite in the form of cold and brooding, Lucille knows that her kindness and her ability to see the good In everyone is going to outweigh a certain someone’s view on life. But forbidden is a drug and temptation is it’s partner.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=34p02km" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491235075i/22388498._SX540_.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Graham has a lot of issues. I won’t even try to sugar coat his past and how he perceives everyone else around him because I cant. He doesn’t trust easily and he’s okay with not having love in his life. Following in his father’s footsteps, Graham has achieved the highest level in excellence and is one of the best mystery/crime authors of his time and if you were to ask him if he would ever want anything else, his answer would be no. <br><br>You see here’s the thing about life. One minute your completely content with something and the next, something or someone just storms in like a hurricane making you wish for more. Making you want to be want to be different. Making you want to feel. And that someone came in the form of a free spirit.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2m2964m" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492031290ra/22475444.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> <i> “That was the thing about hearts- when you thought they were completely full, you somehow found room to add a little more love.”</i></b>  <br><br>I have to say that for the first half of the story, it took me a while to get into. Maybe it was just me and how I was feeling at that time but I wasn’t too invested in everything but the minute I hit the second half, I practically heard the clicking of the final puzzle piece and everything came together. I loved how Graham and Lucille were with one another and how their connection and interactions felt effortless. They certainly had their work cut out for them but I liked how they knew the odds were against them and they still managed to find that peace of balance and never forgot who they were. <br><br>As a fan of this series, I cannot tell you how much I loved reading about these complex and loving characters. This is a bittersweet moment and I’m quite sad that this is the last book in the series but you know what they say: All good things must come to an end.<br><br> And oh how good this was….<br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=287zt5j" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480190806i/21283423._SX540_.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://chatterbooksbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480142939i/21277960.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.facebook.com/chatterbooksbookblog/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480142939i/21277961.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/chatterbooksbookblog8984/?hl=en" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480142939i/21277962.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="mailto:chatterbooksbookblog@gmail.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1962716458" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14362525444528952718">★★★ <b>3.5 Stars</b> ★★★<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"We weren’t supposed to feel this way. We weren’t supposed to fall for one another, she and I. Yet it seemed gravity had a way of pulling us closer."</b>
</blockquote><br/>This was a genuinely lovely story, it was somewhat unique, and had strong likeable characters with a decent plotline.<br/><br/>Our heroine Lucy is a free-spirited, quirky lady who wears her heart on her sleeve. She has two sisters, one that she is very close to, and another that she has reluctantly drifted apart from. The relationship bet</span>
  <span id="freeText14362525444528952718" style="display:none">★★★ <b>3.5 Stars</b> ★★★<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"We weren’t supposed to feel this way. We weren’t supposed to fall for one another, she and I. Yet it seemed gravity had a way of pulling us closer."</b>
</blockquote><br>This was a genuinely lovely story, it was somewhat unique, and had strong likeable characters with a decent plotline.<br><br>Our heroine Lucy is a free-spirited, quirky lady who wears her heart on her sleeve. She has two sisters, one that she is very close to, and another that she has reluctantly drifted apart from. The relationship between the three sisters forms a very large part of this story.<br><br>Then we have our broody hero, Graham. He is the polar opposite to Lucy, he finds it hard to love and doesn't let too many get close to him and his abandonment issues cause him great loneliness.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all."</b>
</blockquote><br>I loved how they came to meet, and how their lives merged by circumstance, it was an interesting mix of angst and emotional.<br><br>I felt the ending was slightly rushed and it wasn't my favourite out of the four Elements books, but it was most definitely a book worth reading, and I just love Brittainy's beautiful words.<br><br><b>The Gravity of Us is a standalone contemporary romance, told from dual POV.<b><br><br><i>ARC gratefully received</i><br><br> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilovebooklove" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img <div id="review_1984479451" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1984479451" />
    <a title="DW" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40762852-dw"><img alt="DW" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536259397p2/40762852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1984479451?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="DW" class="user" itemprop="url" name="DW" href="/user/show/40762852-dw">DW</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40762852-dw?shelf=elements">elements</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1984479451" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16830861008418468953">The Gravity Of Us was such a lovely story. It deserves all the stars and more. <br/><br/>For me.. This was everything that I needed. I have been in a bit of a reading funk lately and this pulled me right on out, giving me all the feels. <br/><br/>I pretty well know that when I start a Brittainy Cherry book, I am going to fall apart, be put back together, fall apart again and then put back together again. It's a vicious cycle but I love it anyway. I am even going to say that this is probably my favorite of her books</span>
  <span id="freeText16830861008418468953" style="display:none">The Gravity Of Us was such a lovely story. It deserves all the stars and more. <br /><br />For me.. This was everything that I needed. I have been in a bit of a reading funk lately and this pulled me right on out, giving me all the feels. <br /><br />I pretty well know that when I start a Brittainy Cherry book, I am going to fall apart, be put back together, fall apart again and then put back together again. It's a vicious cycle but I love it anyway. I am even going to say that this is probably my favorite of her books that I have read so far. <br /><br />Graham Russell (Graham Cracker) was such a broken man. He was rude and hard. <br />He didn't trust people and lived a miserable life. <br /><br />Lucy was the complete opposite. She was full of life, always happy and loved with her whole heart. She lived a bit of a hippy life. She drove Graham crazy with her upbeat personality. That was probably my favorite part. <br /><br /><br />It's not an easy book to review for me because there are so many emotions and I just don't know where to begin. I loved it 100%. <br /><br />My favorites:<br /><br /><b>She was the girl who felt everything, and I was the man who felt nothing at all.<br /><br />“You’re both hot and cold all at once, and I cannot for the life of me figure you out. I don’t know how to read you, Graham Russell. I pride myself on being able to read people, but you are different.”<br /><br />“Just because you smile and act free doesn’t mean the cage doesn’t exist. It merely means you lowered your standards for how far you’ll allow yourself to fly.” <br /><br />“I tried to list the things I find pleasant, outside of Talon of course. It’s a short list, really, only two things so far, and oddly enough, it begins and ends with you.”<br /><br />It’s you,” I whispered, our lips still slightly touching. “My greatest hope is, and always will be, you.”<br /><br />As we lay there that night, I thought about our story. How she found me when I was lost, how she saved me when I needed her the most. How she forced me to stop pushing people away and proved to me that real love wasn’t something from fairytale books. She taught me that real love took time. Real love took work. Real love took communication. Real love only grew if those involved took the time to nurture it, to water it, to give it light.<br /><br /><br />Such a beautiful story!! ❤️</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16830861008418468953" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KgRVczmqR+RUkCClKWyDAd1gRKWMKmnoOM33CJ7yj223YOr+h8VYmHVkQDy/E9iaH+ehsDb2w1gD21vfxaBk8A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zFDLOudXdJJ5SZ04zMD7Tj1VhDyZWTWczbGSk643Z6FRNHS3WThr7li9/aFav6DV/9JhKSOFnyz2pz5E9WWMPA==')})
  }

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/52922245-the-gravity-of-us">Quotes from The Gravity of Us</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;If you need to fall, fall into me.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/8459095-if-you-need-to-fall-fall-into-me">94 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Loneliness is a liar,” Graham told me, sitting down on the edge of his bed as he spoke. “It’s toxic and deadly most of the time. It forces people to believe they are better off with the devil himself than being alone, because somehow being alone means a person failed. Somehow being alone means a person isn’t good enough. So, more often than not, the poison of loneliness seeps in and makes a person believe that any kind of attention must stand for love. Fake love that is built on a bed of loneliness will fail—I should know. I’ve been alone all my life.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/8463419-loneliness-is-a-liar-graham-told-me-sitting-down-on">62 likes</a>
